        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible BigMomPiratesColors" style="color: var(--colorscheme-txt, var(--pi-txt-fallback));">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: var(--colorscheme-bg, var(--pi-bg-fallback))">Devil Fruit</th></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">Mochi Mochi no Mi</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Mochi-Mochi Fruit</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Mochi; Springy</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia#Special_Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Special Paramecia</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><b>Charlotte Katakuri</b> is the second son and third child of the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a><sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">[3]</a></sup> and the elder triplet brother of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Daifuku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Oven</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-5">[5]</a></sup> He is also one of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Three_Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Three Sweet Commanders</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a><sup id="cite_ref-mention_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mention-4">[4]</a></sup> and serves as <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>'s <b>Minister of Flour</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">粉大臣</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kona Daijin</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, governing over <a href="/wiki/Komugi_Island" title="Komugi Island">Komugi Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his actions and role, Katakuri is the secondary antagonist in the second half of the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Arc" title="Whole Cake Island Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</a>. He, alongside his younger siblings <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> and Oven, become temporary and reluctant allies of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> during <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Film:_Red" title="One Piece Film: Red"><i>One Piece Film: Red</i></a>.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">

	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8438" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the height of Charlotte Katakuri?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In the One Piece universe, Charlotte Katakuri is an extremely tall character with a height of 509 cm or 16'8½". He is nearly triple the height of Monkey D. Luffy and is marginally taller than his triplet brothers, Charlotte Daifuku and Charlotte Oven.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>

				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How old is Charlotte Katakuri in the series?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In the series, Charlotte Katakuri, affiliated with the Charlotte Family and Big Mom Pirates, is 48 years old.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>

			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8440" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the current status of Katakuri in the series, is he dead or alive?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Charlotte Katakuri's status in the series is not specified in the given context. Nonetheless, there's no evidence suggesting he's deceased. Katakuri is recognized for his serious demeanor, his commitment to safeguarding his family and crew, and his proficient use of Kenbunshoku Haki to preemptively tackle potential issues or dangers.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>

			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8441" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of doughnuts in Katakuri's character development?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Charlotte Katakuri's character development is deeply tied to doughnuts. His childhood love for doughnuts led to his mouth's expansion due to frequent eating. Consuming doughnuts induces a state of bliss in Katakuri, enjoyed privately during his merienda. His combat techniques also incorporate doughnuts, as he shapes mochi into their form. This illustrates the intricacy of his character.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span></h2>
<p>Katakuri is an extremely tall, large and muscular man standing in at 509 cm <sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-5">[5]</a></sup> where he stands at nearly three times <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s height and is slightly taller than his younger triplet brothers, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a>, who are incredibly tall themselves. He has short spiky crimson hair (pinkish crimson in the manga/anime) and two symmetric scars on both sides of his face. He has long legs with his thighs being equally as long as his lower limbs.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">[3]</a></sup> His mouth, which is usually covered up, contains sharp <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pelican_eel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pelican eel">Pelican eel</a>-like teeth and is capable of expanding to an enormous size.<sup id="cite_ref-c883a_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883a-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri has sharp and intense crimson eyes, highly arched eyebrows and prominent lower eyelashes under each eye. He wears a massive light feather ragged scarf that covers his mouth and reaches his shoulders. He also wears a torn leather vest with "<b>CHARLOTTE</b>" on the back that exposes most of his torso, dark gloves and pants, a belt with a skull-shaped buckle and spiked boots with spurs. His torso is very defined, having prominent abdominal muscles covered in pink tattoos and he wears spiked bracelets on his arms as well as knee pads with a single spike on them.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, Katakuri wore a dark cloak when arriving at the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-e825_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-e825-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p>As a child, Katakuri wore a dark torn jacket and dark pants without a scarf. It was only after <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> was attacked that he decided to cover his mouth.<sup id="cite_ref-c893a_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893a-9">[9]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span></h2>
<p>Katakuri is a calm, serious and diligent man who devotes himself to protecting <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">his family</a> and crew and achieving their objectives. He frequently uses his advanced <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a> to quickly address any problems or threats that he foresees, and whenever possible he will work to change the future he foresees and stop the problem before it happens.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> Katakuri makes sure to waste no time in accomplishing his tasks; when his older brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> was gloating to the captured <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>, Katakuri told him to hurry and shoot them immediately.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> Katakuri is quite brutal when attacking opponents to ensure they are quickly neutralized and will use his weapons to inflict gruesome wounds with impunity.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> Katakuri's haste to resolve problems can sometimes work against him, though, as his attempts to change the future may not achieve his intended result.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup> Katakuri is almost always calm even in the most perilous of situations, as it is necessary for his mind to be clear in order to utilize Observation Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> If he is taken by surprise or foresees something terrible in the future, he is shown to lose color on his face and he may sometimes shout, but he does not panic.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p><p>When it comes to judging his opponent's power, Katakuri is neither boastful nor meek and so will bluntly point out when an opponent is clearly inferior to him (to the point of encouraging them to flee while they can) <sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c888_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c888-16">[16]</a></sup> but will also notice if they pose a serious threat or are improving their abilities <sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> and he will even commend enemies who demonstrate impressive strength or tactical maneuvers.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> He takes care to never underestimate his opponents' abilities, and rather than entertain the activation of a new ability he is quite pragmatic and will prevent his opponent from activating it.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> Even when his crewmates were confident that the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> would be killed by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> before they could escape to their ship the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Katakuri took forces to lie in wait on the Sunny "just in case."<sup id="cite_ref-c874_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c874-21">[21]</a></sup> Katakuri also takes note of opponents' potential, and will specifically target enemies whom he feels could pose a more serious threat in the future.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri takes his status as the strongest subordinate of Big Mom quite seriously and makes the effort to maintain the appearance of perfection that his siblings and crewmates consider him to have, particularly by never lying on his back in public.<sup id="cite_ref-c902a_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902a-23">[23]</a></sup> However, he has been shown to silence siblings who are heaping excessive amounts of praise onto him.<sup id="cite_ref-c882a_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882a-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png/revision/latest?cb=20190113102441" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Matchs Luffy's Wound" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri Matchs Luffy's Wound.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190113102441"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png/revision/latest?cb=20190113102441" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Matchs Luffy's Wound" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190113102441" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri Matchs Luffy's Wound.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190113102441"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_Matchs_Luffy%27s_Wound.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri wounds himself to be on par with Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although he works to eliminate enemies efficiently, Katakuri is ultimately an honorable fighter who prefers to fight fairly and heavily respects opponents who can match him. Thus, he absolutely despises receiving unwanted assistance in a fight between men and will even yell at a sibling if they interfere in his battles. If he finds that he inflicted a wound on someone due to outside assistance, he will give his own body the same wound to compensate for it and even the playing field.<sup id="cite_ref-c893b_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893b-26">[26]</a></sup> He even apologies his enemy for not having a genuine fight. When he was bested in combat for the first time by Luffy, Katakuri retained his respect for the pirate and was enthused, rather than angry, when Luffy confirmed his intention of coming back and defeating Big Mom in the future.<sup id="cite_ref-c896_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-27">[27]</a></sup> Later, he even smiled after learning that Luffy had escaped from <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c902a_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902a-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702142053" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Gluttony" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri's Gluttony.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702142053"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702142053" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Gluttony" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702142053" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri's Gluttony.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e2/Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702142053"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri%27s_Gluttony.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri's private merienda time, where he gorges on doughnuts and tea in gluttonous bliss.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>To cope with the stresses of his position, Katakuri takes regular light meal breaks, known as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Merienda" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Merienda">Merienda</a> where he feasts on his favorite food of doughnuts and drinks tea. Katakuri has loved doughnuts since he was a child, to the point of eating them so often that he caused his mouth to artificially expand.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> Eating doughnuts puts Katakuri in a state of bliss, and during his merienda he has been shown voicing his love for them out loud in very intimate language. Katakuri keeps his merienda extremely private as he lies on his back and relaxes during it, which is a stark contrast to his siblings' view of him as someone who never lies down. The merienda is a very important part of Katakuri's routine and so he will become quite annoyed if something keeps him from doing it at the allotted time. When his fight with Luffy made his merienda late, Katakuri became willing to forgo his usual diligence and attempted to quickly finish off his opponent by burying him in mochi, not taking the time to make sure Luffy had died. <sup id="cite_ref-c883b_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883b-28">[28]</a></sup>
</p><p>Another reason that Katakuri shrouds his merienda in utmost secrecy is that he is extremely sensitive about his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pelican_eel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pelican eel">Pelican eel</a>-like mouth, which he was bullied for as a child. Initially, he had no issue with just attacking his bullies in response, but after the bullies took revenge by attacking his younger sister <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a>, Katakuri took to wearing a scarf, covering his mouth at all times in public.<sup id="cite_ref-c902a_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902a-23">[23]</a></sup> When his cooks accidentally saw his mouth in the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>, Katakuri completely lost his mind and used brutal force against them with murderous intent; he was so angry that he even misheard one of their pleas as a comment about his mouth.<sup id="cite_ref-c883b_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883b-28">[28]</a></sup> However, Katakuri went on to take off his mouth covering during his fight with Luffy after acknowledging the latter as an equal, believing that Luffy was no more deserving of Flampe's scorn than he was.<sup id="cite_ref-c893b_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893b-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri has a habit of telling people around him what he foresees them saying or doing next.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> This habit ended up backfiring on him during his fight with Luffy as his vocal premonition of Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a> deactivating gave Luffy the chance to fly away from him before it did.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</span></h4>
<p>Katakuri is shown to be fiercely loyal to his <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">mother</a> as he would not hesitate to eliminate anyone who would threaten her.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> He supported Linlin's ambitions as shown when he attempted to kill <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> to begin her plan to assassinate the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>. When the wedding ceremony was about to get hectic, Katakuri immediately leaped in front of his mother to protect her from harm.<sup id="cite_ref-c862_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c862-30">[30]</a></sup> He is aware of Linlin's attachment to <a href="/wiki/Carmel" title="Carmel">Carmel</a>'s portrait and did everything he could to prevent its destruction. Despite his loyalty and devotion to her, Linlin sees Katakuri as a lowly child of hers and will not tolerate him interfering with her business. Katakuri merely accepts being patronized by his mother but will also explain himself to her as shown when he provided his reason for attacking <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c863_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> attempted to attack his mother with <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">Big Father</a>'s cannons, Katakuri clogged up the cannon barrels with mochi, effectively protecting Big Mom while she was vulnerable.<sup id="cite_ref-c869a_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869a-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his loyalty towards his mother, when Katakuri questioned Luffy about him becoming strong enough to defeat her, Katakuri wished Luffy the best of luck in his quest.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Siblings">Siblings</span></h4>
<p>Due to his caring nature, Katakuri is very close with a majority to almost all of his siblings as he provided them with earplugs after they were incapacitated by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s screams.<sup id="cite_ref-c868a_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868a-33">[33]</a></sup> Katakuri is always prompted to save his siblings if they are in danger. He saved his younger half-sister <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Galette" title="Charlotte Galette">Charlotte Galette</a> from falling after the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a> collapsed as she called desperately for him.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup> He also showed concern for his older half-brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> after he was caught in an explosion.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> He also prevented <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> from attacking <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Mascarpone" title="Charlotte Mascarpone">Charlotte Mascarpone</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Joscarpone" title="Charlotte Joscarpone">Charlotte Joscarpone</a>, calling them his precious siblings. He also seemed relieved to learn that Perospero survived the explosion caused by <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c880_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c880-36">[36]</a></sup> Katakuri's strength was held with such immense respect and admiration among his siblings that they never fathomed the possibility that he could lose in battle as they were in utter disbelief and complete rage when <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> revealed that Luffy defeated him and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a> was enraged that his oldest triplet brother's unbeatable record was broken and tried to kill Luffy, only to fail several times due to the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c898_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c898-37">[37]</a></sup>
</p><p>During their childhood, after Katakuri beat up some bullies who ridiculed his mouth, they took their revenge on Brûlée, scarring her face. Brûlée did not hold any grudge against Katakuri, saying that he was fine the way he is. After unleashing his own revenge, Katakuri started hiding his face to protect his family.<sup id="cite_ref-c902b_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902b-38">[38]</a></sup> After the Sanji Retrieval Team crashed the tea party, he saved Brûlée from her captors though he did hold her in a threatening way after pointing out how her captors used her powers but listened to her pleas of being a hostage.<sup id="cite_ref-c869b_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869b-39">[39]</a></sup> He acted similarly when Luffy attacked Brûlée, protecting her without hesitation. He even warned Luffy to not dare lay a hand on his sister, showing a strong determination to protect her. Brûlée holds Katakuri's strength in high regard as she proudly bragged about it to Luffy while the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat</a> captain was struggling in his fight against the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Three_Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Sweet Commander</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c882b_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882b-40">[40]</a></sup> After Katakuri was defeated, Brûlée was deeply upset and furious with Luffy and she later tended to her half-brother's wounds. During their talk, it was shown that they have an understanding of each other as Brúlée speculated that Katakuri had fallen willingly on his back, which led to Katakuri confessing that his perfect image was nothing but a lie. When Katakuri asked about Luffy, Brúlée guessed that he would be pleased to know that Luffy escaped <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>. Katakuri smirked, confirming her assumption.<sup id="cite_ref-c902a_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902a-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Flampe" title="Charlotte Flampe">Charlotte Flampe</a> once deeply admired Katakuri and she stated that all of his little half-sisters have selected him as their favorite brother and that he is also beloved by his fellow brothers. She meddled in his fight with Luffy, wanting to preserve her brother's perfect status and become his favorite little sister.<sup id="cite_ref-c891_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c891-41">[41]</a></sup> However, when Katakuri caught Flampe's interruption, he went to her and angrily berated her for her meddling actions after stabbing himself with his trident and revealing his entire face to her.<sup id="cite_ref-c893b_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893b-26">[26]</a></sup> Flampe's opinion of him immediately turned negative and she even threatened to expose his secret, after which Katakuri willingly knocked her out with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> so he could have a fair fight with Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> Some of Katakuri's siblings, such as Perospero, Oven, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> and Brûlée, are already aware of his eel-like mouth, but they never scorned him for it.
</p><p>When discussing who should succeed Big Mom in case she was killed, Daifuku believed that Katakuri should be her successor.<sup id="cite_ref-c934_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c934-43">[43]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Subordinates">Subordinates</span></h3>
<p>Outside of his family members, Katakuri also seems to care for the safety of his subordinates as he ordered the Chess Soldiers to return to the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a> since he foresaw that they would have suffered a swift and complete beating from <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> had they remained.<sup id="cite_ref-c877a_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877a-44">[44]</a></sup> As the strongest of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Three_Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Three Sweet Commanders</a> who exemplifies the image of a dignified and level-headed warrior, he commands great respect and admiration from his subordinates.<sup id="cite_ref-c879a_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879a-45">[45]</a></sup> He acts forgiving to their discrepancies to his perfectionist attitude, as he accommodated to his black tea cooling down due to his battle with Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c883c_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883c-46">[46]</a></sup>
</p><p>While seemingly a strong leader who respects his subordinates in turn, Katakuri goes to great lengths to keep this image and he keeps his true face out of their sight, eating in solitude. Believing he was eating in a dignified manner to recuperate his nutrition, the patisseries who delivered Katakuri his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Merienda" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Merienda">Merienda</a> became utterly shocked when they inadvertently witnessed his gluttonous and slothful eating manners, shattering their vision of his perfect warrior image. Once exposed, Katakuri brutally executed the chefs and even misinterpreted one of their pleas as a comment to his mouth, which resulted in him acting even more violent towards them.<sup id="cite_ref-c883d_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883d-47">[47]</a></sup> However, despite this previous demeanor, Katakuri did not mind showing his full face to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Flampe" title="Charlotte Flampe">Charlotte Flampe</a> and his fan club and he was content at just knocking them out, knowing full well that they were going to expose his secret.
</p><p>Upon hearing of Katakuri's defeat at the hands of Luffy, the crew stationed outside of the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a> were furious and tried to kill Luffy in revenge, incorrectly accusing him of using underhanded methods to win.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Capone_Bege">Capone Bege</span></h4>
<p>Initially, Katakuri seemed very respectful towards <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> as he prevented two of the latter's crewmates from being killed by <a href="/wiki/Jigra" title="Jigra">Jigra</a> before the ceremony. However, their encounter quickly becomes standoffish when Bege questioned the reasoning behind Katakuri's actions. As Katakuri explained his reason for killing Jigra, he also reminded Bege of his rank as a Rook.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> When the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> caused trouble for the wedding, Bege pinned Luffy down before noticing that Katakuri had foreseen a terrible future. When the Sweet Commander ordered him to kill Luffy, Bege refused and instead ordered his allies to put in their earplugs to avoid Big Mom's screams.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-48">[48]</a></sup> Katakuri realized Bege's betrayal when he attempted to shoot him, but he was unharmed.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup> He tried but failed to prevent Luffy from showing <a href="/wiki/Carmel" title="Carmel">Carmel</a>'s broken picture to Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c865_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c865-50">[50]</a></sup> After Bege's assassination attempt on Big Mom failed, Katakuri created earplugs for his siblings, enabling them to regain their composure,<sup id="cite_ref-c868a_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868a-33">[33]</a></sup> which forced Bege to transform into a <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">giant fortress</a> to save himself and his allies.<sup id="cite_ref-c868b_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868b-51">[51]</a></sup> As <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> was helping Bege and his allies escape, Katakuri tried to stop them.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-52">[52]</a></sup> After Bege and his allies successfully escaped the castle, Katakuri immediately formed a team to pursue them.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-53">[53]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sanji_Retrieval_Team">Sanji Retrieval Team</span></h4>
<p>Katakuri made an enemy out of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> when he attempted to kill <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> himself after he foresaw <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a>'s failure in her task and Sanji dodging the priest's shot. However, his own attempt on Sanji's life failed, earning him a glare from the Straw Hat Cook and the only thing he could do next was to prepare for the chaos caused by the <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">duplicates</a> of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c862_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c862-30">[30]</a></sup> After Bege's assassination attempt on Big Mom failed, Katakuri assisted his siblings in cornering the Straw Hats and their allies.<sup id="cite_ref-c868a_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868a-33">[33]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c868b_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868b-51">[51]</a></sup> As Caesar was helping the Straw Hats escape the venue, Katakuri wasted no time in hindering their escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-52">[52]</a></sup> After the Straw Hats and their allies successfully escaped the castle, Katakuri immediately assembled groups and planned to pursue them.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-53">[53]</a></sup> Along with his brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>, he was confronted by <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a> when they returned to the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c875_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c875-54">[54]</a></sup> As Chopper and Brook fought to retake the Sunny, Katakuri simply complimented Brook for his strength.<sup id="cite_ref-c876_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c876-55">[55]</a></sup> When the rest of the crew returned, Katakuri was not surprised. After <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> severely injured Perospero in a suicide explosion, Katakuri tried to prevent the Straw Hats' escape until Luffy pulled him into the Mirro-World.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Katakuri_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20180925230400" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri and Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="342" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri and Luffy.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_and_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Katakuri_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180925230400"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Katakuri_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20180925230400" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri and Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Katakuri_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180925230400" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="342" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri and Luffy.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_and_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Katakuri_and_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180925230400"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_and_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri towering over Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Tea_Party" title="Tea Party">Tea Party</a>, Katakuri was a huge hindrance to <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s efforts to facilitate <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>'s assassination plan as he tried to stop Luffy from exploiting <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s weakness.<sup id="cite_ref-c863_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863-31">[31]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c865_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c865-50">[50]</a></sup>
</p><p>After Luffy and his group escaped the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a>, Katakuri led a pursuit team after them, swearing to personally eliminate Luffy before he can become a threat to his mother<sup id="cite_ref-c873_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c873-56">[56]</a></sup> and later insisted on staying on the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Straw Hat's ship</a> to ambush them just in case they escaped his mother.<sup id="cite_ref-c874_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c874-21">[21]</a></sup>
</p><p>After Luffy dragged him into the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a> to keep him from preventing his friends' escape, the two fought each other in a fearsome clash.<sup id="cite_ref-c878_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c878-57">[57]</a></sup> Initially, Katakuri was patronizing and informative towards Luffy's many efforts to defeat him.<sup id="cite_ref-c879b_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879b-58">[58]</a></sup> Despite believing that Luffy had no chance of defeating him, he developed some respect for Luffy as he remarked on Luffy's skill in his dodging that resorted to Katakuri using his awakened powers.<sup id="cite_ref-c882c_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882c-59">[59]</a></sup> Though he claimed that he was not underestimating Luffy, he failed to properly finish off Luffy before indulging himself with sweets. However, after Luffy interrupted his snack time and exposed his face as well as his sloppy eating manners,<sup id="cite_ref-c883c_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883c-46">[46]</a></sup> Katakuri regretted not making sure Luffy was dead. Enraged, Katakuri resumed his attempt to kill Luffy for good. However, in his anger, Luffy was able to hit him and Katakuri challenged Luffy's claim of finding out his weakness.<sup id="cite_ref-c883e_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883e-60">[60]</a></sup> When Luffy briefly gained the upper hand, Katakuri's respect for him seems to have grown as he commended Luffy for being able to injure him and commented that he understood how he was able to overcome his younger brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Cracker" title="Charlotte Cracker">Charlotte Cracker</a>. However, after he disrupted Luffy's attacks, he promised to not allow him to gain the advantage again.<sup id="cite_ref-c884_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c884-61">[61]</a></sup> When Luffy retreated from the battle due to the time limit of his <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a>, Katakuri pursued him, not willing to let him get away, but Luffy managed to escape the Mirro-World before Katakuri could catch him.<sup id="cite_ref-c885_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c885-62">[62]</a></sup> While he was resting, Luffy declared his intention to surpass Katakuri and later returned to confront him again as the latter was impressed by his bravery.<sup id="cite_ref-c886_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c886-63">[63]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c888_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c888-16">[16]</a></sup> He also seems to be worried about Luffy's potential as he was shaken by the thought of the latter achieving his level of <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a> and tried his best to finish the fight quickly.<sup id="cite_ref-c892_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c892-64">[64]</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">

  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">I no longer...think that you're below my level.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
