  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Katakuri acknowledging Luffy as his equal in their fight.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p>As they fought, Katakuri's opinion of Luffy would eventually grow with respect into that of a rivalry. Even though he wanted to end Luffy before he could become a threat, Katakuri wanted to defeat him honorably as shown when he disapproved of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Flampe" title="Charlotte Flampe">Charlotte Flampe</a>'s meddling and even injured himself to make the fight fairer.<sup id="cite_ref-c893b_26-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893b-26">[26]</a></sup> He even apologized to his enemy for his sister's actions as they use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> to knock out Flampe and her subordinates as punishment. As they resumed their battle, Katakuri told Luffy that he no longer saw him as below his level.<sup id="cite_ref-c893c_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893c-66">[66]</a></sup> At the end of their clash, Katakuri failed in his promise to kill Luffy as the latter defeated him. Afterward, Katakuri briefly stood up to talk with Luffy who told him that he'd return to beat Big Mom and become Pirate King and Katakuri, believing Luffy, wished him good luck in his dream before losing consciousness. As he laid beaten, Luffy showed some respect to his downed adversary by covering his mouth with his extra hat before leaving.<sup id="cite_ref-c896_27-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-27">[27]</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> informed him that Luffy escaped <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>, Katakuri smiled at the news and now recognized Luffy as a competent fighter.<sup id="cite_ref-c902a_23-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902a-23">[23]</a></sup> Instead of giving a nickname, Luffy calls Katakuri by his name.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vinsmoke_Family">Vinsmoke Family</span></h4>
<p>Since Katakuri took part in <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s plan to assassinate the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>, he is an enemy of the family. His failed attempt to kill <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> alerted the family of Big Mom's treachery though they were restrained before they could do anything.<sup id="cite_ref-c862_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c862-30">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> As the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> were causing chaos at the wedding, Katakuri told his <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">elder brother</a> to kill the Vinsmokes immediately, which ended up in failure.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> When the Vinsmokes fought against the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> to help the Straw Hats and <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a> escape from the wedding venue, Katakuri easily defeated <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Vinsmoke Ichiji</a> in combat. However, he was prevented from killing him due to the destruction of the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-52">[52]</a></sup> After the Vinsmoke Family and their allies escaped from Big Mom's castle, Katakuri formed three pursuit teams to chase them.<sup id="cite_ref-c873_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c873-56">[56]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span></h2>
<p>As one of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Three_Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Three Sweet Commanders</a>, Katakuri's authority in the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> is second only to his <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">mother</a>'s, and as <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>'s Minister of Flour, he holds authority over <a href="/wiki/Komugi_Island" title="Komugi Island">Komugi Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_5-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p><p>In battle, Katakuri is a very powerful combatant. His tremendous bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>1,057,000,000 shows how dangerous he is considered by the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a><sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">[3]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> of the infamous <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> has likewise declared him a monstrous threat.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> According to his crewmates, Katakuri is the strongest of the Three Sweet Commanders,<sup id="cite_ref-c879a_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879a-45">[45]</a></sup> the strongest of Big Mom's children overall<sup id="cite_ref-c882a_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882a-24">[24]</a></sup> and thus the most capable member of their crew aside from Big Mom herself; <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> even stated that if Big Mom were to die, Katakuri's skills would make him the worthiest of succeeding her as captain of the Big Mom Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c934_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c934-43">[43]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri has been called a "monster" for his strength ever since he was a child,<sup id="cite_ref-c893a_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893a-9">[9]</a></sup> and until his first loss against <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, he was said to have never lost a single battle throughout his life—his long and perfect record of victory described by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a> as "legendary".<sup id="cite_ref-c898_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c898-37">[37]</a></sup>
</p><p>Also, Katakuri is strong-willed as he withstood a blast of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> long enough to continue on his feet to help his siblings.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Katakuri_Gatling.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172939" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Gatling" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri Gatling.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Gatling.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Katakuri_Gatling.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172939"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Katakuri_Gatling.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172939" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Gatling" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Katakuri_Gatling.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172939" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri Gatling.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Gatling.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Katakuri_Gatling.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172939"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_Gatling.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri's similar fighting style to Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Noted to be the strongest of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates#Three_Sweet_Commanders" title="Big Mom Pirates">Three Sweet Commanders</a>, Katakuri possesses immense physical strength, being able to flick jellybeans with such extreme force and velocity that they act like bullets, mortally wounding his opponents with a single shot.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> Even from a great distance, Katakuri can kill a man with a flicked jellybean.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> He was also able to defeat <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Vinsmoke Ichiji</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Modified_Humans" title="Modified Humans">genetically enhanced</a> <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a> commander who was wearing his <a href="/wiki/Raid_Suit" title="Raid Suit">Raid Suit</a>, with minimal effort and without incurring any injuries himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-52">[52]</a></sup> Katakuri is an extremely skilled and powerful hand-to-hand combatant. Supplemented with his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> powers, he uses a fighting style similar to <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">Gomu Gomu no Mi</a> techniques and he can counter Luffy's Red Hawk without any effort.<sup id="cite_ref-c877b_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877b-71">[71]</a></sup> With his own version of Luffy's Elephant Gun, he overpowered and badly injured Luffy in a clash of strength.<sup id="cite_ref-c879c_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879c-72">[72]</a></sup> When he performed his <b>Zan Giri Mochi</b> attack, he was able to create a large crater in the ground when he sent Luffy crashing through the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c895_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c895-73">[73]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri is extremely fast and possesses extraordinary reflexes. Due to his speed, an expert <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a> user such as Luffy barely had time to react to his attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-c863_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863-31">[31]</a></sup> He effortlessly subdued the speedy <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">mink</a> <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a>, and kept up with the blinding speed of Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Gear 2</a> attacks, catching the two of them off-guard with swift and powerful kicks.<sup id="cite_ref-c878_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c878-57">[57]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup> He was even able to keep up with Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a> <b><a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques#Snakeman" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Snakeman</a></b> form, and even outpace him at times.<sup id="cite_ref-c895_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c895-73">[73]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri possesses tremendous levels of durability and endurance, being able to withstand multiple immensely powerful attacks from Gear 4 Luffy and quickly recover to counterattack.<sup id="cite_ref-c884_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c884-61">[61]</a></sup> He was able to impale himself with his own spear and showed only minor signs of discomfort.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup> He also has vast reserves of stamina, being able to fight with Luffy non-stop for several hours in the Mirro-World without issue before succumbing to exhaustion only at the very end of the fight.<sup id="cite_ref-c896_27-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-27">[27]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spearmanship">Spearmanship</span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Mogura" title="Mogura">Mogura</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Mogura_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230709155036" class="image"><img alt="Mogura Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="261" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mogura Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mogura_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Mogura_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20230709155036"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Mogura_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230709155036" class="image"><img alt="Mogura Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Mogura_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20230709155036" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="261" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mogura Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mogura_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Mogura_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20230709155036"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mogura_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri wielding Mogura.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri wields a trident named <b>Mogura</b> in battle where he was first seen wielding it during <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a>'s wedding ceremony.<sup id="cite_ref-c862_30-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c862-30">[30]</a></sup> When not in use, he keeps the trident inside his mochi body.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> Katakuri is extremely skilled in wielding his trident, which he uses in conjunction with his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> powers and physical prowess to perform devastating thrusts.<sup id="cite_ref-c882b_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882b-40">[40]</a></sup>
</p><p>When he was younger, he used a trident with a much simpler design.<sup id="cite_ref-c902b_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902b-38">[38]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marksmanship">Marksmanship</span></h3>
<p>Katakuri's immense physical strength and accuracy allow him to act as a sniper and marksman. Katakuri is highly skilled in flicking jelly beans as improvised bullets with great accuracy. Even from a very far distance, he can kill <a href="/wiki/Jigra" title="Jigra">Jigra</a> with a hit in the head from so far away that <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> did not even notice him, and later would have hit <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> as well had the latter not <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">dodged</a> at the last moment.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">Mochi Mochi no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png/revision/latest?cb=20180506061805" class="image"><img alt="Mochi Mochi no Mi Ability" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mochi Mochi no Mi Ability.png" data-image-key="Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180506061805"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png/revision/latest?cb=20180506061805" class="image"><img alt="Mochi Mochi no Mi Ability" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180506061805" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mochi Mochi no Mi Ability.png" data-image-key="Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180506061805"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi_Ability.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Mochi Mochi no Mi in use.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri ate the Mochi Mochi no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia#Special_Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Special Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that lets him create, control and transform his body into mochi at will. His mochi is extremely thick and adhesive, allowing him to trap even extremely strong enemies with it, although it loses its effectiveness when exposed to liquids.<sup id="cite_ref-c863_31-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p><p>He frequently uses these abilities in hand-to-hand combat, sprouting several tendrils of mochi on his body to act as extra fists or legs; he can imbue these tendrils with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> to deliver extremely hard punches and kicks.<sup id="cite_ref-c879d_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879d-77">[77]</a></sup> He is also able to enlarge his mochi limbs to gigantic size and stretch them to increase his attack range. By concentrating and compressing mochi into a single fist, Katakuri is capable of delivering punches of devastating power.<sup id="cite_ref-c879c_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879c-72">[72]</a></sup>
</p><p>He is also very creative when using his fruit, as he created mochi earplugs to protect himself and his <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">siblings</a> from the sound of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s scream,<sup id="cite_ref-c868a_33-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868a-33">[33]</a></sup> and also used mochi to plug up and disable the cannons of Bege's <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">Big Father</a> fortress.<sup id="cite_ref-c869a_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869a-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri can transform his body like a <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a> user to avoid attacks, as shown when he transformed himself into mochi when being struck by <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>'s bullets.<sup id="cite_ref-c865_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c865-50">[50]</a></sup> With the help of his advanced <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>, he is even capable of manipulating his body structure, dodging Haki-imbued attacks and remaining unharmed by opening holes in his body so his opponents attacks just pass through empty air.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Awakening">Awakening</span></h4>
<p>Katakuri has also mastered his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> powers to the point of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit#Awakening" title="Devil Fruit">awakening</a> his Devil Fruit, enabling him to transform nearby inorganic material into mochi, greatly enhancing the range of his attacks and allowing him to manipulate the environment to his advantage.<sup id="cite_ref-c882c_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882c-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Katakuri is one of the very few people in the world who can use all three types of Haki.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Supreme_King_Haki">Supreme King Haki</span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702144938" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's and Luffy's Supreme King Haki Clash" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri's and Luffy's Supreme King Haki Clash.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702144938"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702144938" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's and Luffy's Supreme King Haki Clash" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702144938" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri's and Luffy's Supreme King Haki Clash.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702144938"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri%27s_and_Luffy%27s_Supreme_King_Haki_Clash.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri's burst of Supreme King Haki clashes with Luffy's.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri possessed the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, a rare form of Haki that only one in several million people in the world can use. He is a capable user of it as shown when he released a large burst along with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s own Supreme King Haki in order to knock out <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Flampe" title="Charlotte Flampe">Charlotte Flampe</a> and her subordinates as punishment for their interruption.<sup id="cite_ref-c893c_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893c-66">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png/revision/latest?cb=20180701143920" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Future Sight" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri's Future Sight.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180701143920"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png/revision/latest?cb=20180701143920" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Future Sight" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180701143920" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri's Future Sight.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180701143920"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri%27s_Future_Sight.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri sees into the future.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri has extraordinary mastery of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> specifically its advanced form of "<a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki#Future_Vision" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Future Vision</a>" that allows him to see (as well as listen) a few seconds ahead into the future. He was able to detect and instantly thwart an assassination attempt on <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> and her affiliates that would have been carried out moments later by a vengeful <a href="/wiki/Tea_Party" title="Tea Party">Tea Party</a> invitee; his predictions were shown to be accurate when Katakuri justified his killing of the guest to <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> and knew word for word how the latter would respond to him. He would later repeat this capacity during his one-on-one battle against <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, accurately predicting the latter's intent to keep on fighting and eventually resorting to the use of <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c882c_59-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882c-59">[59]</a></sup> He correctly foresaw <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a> breaking down and crying at the alter during the wedding ceremony and Luffy's intentions to break <a href="/wiki/Carmel" title="Carmel">Carmel</a>'s portrait. Bege recognized him as the greatest obstacle to his own assassination plan.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup> Katakuri can use his precognition to increase the accuracy of his attacks to such a degree that Luffy, who is a highly skilled Observation Haki user himself, could barely dodge his assaults.
</p><p>The future events Katakuri sees can be changed, which he often attempts to do so himself, as shown when he prevented <a href="/wiki/Jigra" title="Jigra">Jigra</a> from carrying out the assassination plot he foresaw. However, changing the future may not solve anything, or may even make things worse, as shown when he tried to shoot <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>. Other people are also capable of changing the foreseen future.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-48">[48]</a></sup> Also, he is only able to perceive the future from his own senses, as he was confused as to why Pudding was crying at the altar because he was too far away to hear what was about to be said.<sup id="cite_ref-c862_30-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c862-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702155226" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Logia-Like Effect" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri's Logia-Like Effect.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155226"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702155226" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Logia-Like Effect" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155226" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri's Logia-Like Effect.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155226"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri%27s_Logia-Like_Effect.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri's advanced Observation Haki allows him to morph his mochi body to avoid contact.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri can use his Haki in conjunction with his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> power to great effect. Since he can see slightly into the future, he can predict precisely where an attack will land, allowing him time to reshape his mochi body out of harm's way, making attacks simply pass through empty air. Since he is physically dodging the attack and preventing it from coming into contact with him in the first place, even attacks imbued with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> will pass through him without harming him. With this ability, Katakuri is nearly untouchable and he has stated that it had been years since someone laid a hand on him before Luffy managed to do so. Katakuri's Haki can only be nullified if he stops being calm and collected,<sup id="cite_ref-c884_61-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c884-61">[61]</a></sup> or if he faces an opponent whose level of Observation Haki rivals or surpasses his own.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20210828222129" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Flame Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="200" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri's Flame Haki.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210828222129"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20210828222129" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Flame Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210828222129" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="200" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri's Flame Haki.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f7/Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210828222129"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri%27s_Flame_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri's Armament Haki taking the shape of flames.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri is an extremely skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> as shown when he hardened his mochi leg in order to bludgeon and injure <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c863_31-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863-31">[31]</a></sup> His <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a> enhanced strikes are powerful enough to counter and overpower Luffy's own Haki enhanced attacks,<sup id="cite_ref-c879d_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879d-77">[77]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c879c_72-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879c-72">[72]</a></sup> and he has boasted that his Armament Haki is superior to Luffy's.<sup id="cite_ref-c883f_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883f-79">[79]</a></sup> When performing his <b>Zan Giri Mochi</b> attack, Katakuri's Haki becomes flame-shaped, like <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s Haki and Luffy's Haki when he uses <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a> and the luster of it is blue.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Katakuri%27s_Past.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702155305" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Past" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="139" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri's Past.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Past.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Katakuri%27s_Past.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155305"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Katakuri%27s_Past.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702155305" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri's Past" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Katakuri%27s_Past.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155305" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="139" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri's Past.png" data-image-key="Katakuri%27s_Past.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Katakuri%27s_Past.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155305"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri%27s_Past.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri being shunned as a child.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Katakuri was born somewhere on the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> on a boat as the second son of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a> and the third child of the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c891_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c891-41">[41]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> Along with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a>, they make up a set of triplets with Katakuri being the oldest of the three.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs87_5-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs87-5">[5]</a></sup> At the age of two, Katakuri tasted doughnuts for the first time and it became his favorite food.
</p><p>At the age of three, Katakuri's fast eating habits caused the size of his mouth to expand greatly and tore his cheeks apart, leaving deep scars on the sides of his mouth.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> As a result, he was shunned and ostracized by others due to his appearance, but he was strong enough to fend off his bullies, making them run away in fear.<sup id="cite_ref-c893a_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c893a-9">[9]</a></sup> Some of his siblings such as <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a>, Oven, Daifuku and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> do not scorn him, although Perospero once told Katakuri that he would be able to make friends if he hid his eel-like mouth. When Katakuri was five, he obtained and ate the <a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">Mochi Mochi no Mi</a> <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup>
</p><p>When he was ten years old, some bullies that Katakuri beat up took revenge by cutting Brûlée's face. Angered, Katakuri retaliated and attacked the bullies. Having blamed his naivete for the attack on Brûlée, Katakuri decided to become a ruthless and cold man to make everyone fear him so he could protect his siblings and family, which included hiding his mouth with a scarf since then.<sup id="cite_ref-c902b_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902b-38">[38]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</span></h4>
<p>On the day before the wedding of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, Katakuri and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Smoothie" title="Charlotte Smoothie">Charlotte Smoothie</a> reported to the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-mention_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mention-4">[4]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Jigra%27s_Death.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702155459" class="image"><img alt="Jigra's Death" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jigra's Death.png" data-image-key="Jigra%27s_Death.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Jigra%27s_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155459"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Jigra%27s_Death.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702155459" class="image"><img alt="Jigra's Death" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Jigra%27s_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155459" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jigra's Death.png" data-image-key="Jigra%27s_Death.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/79/Jigra%27s_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702155459"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jigra%27s_Death.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri shoots Jigra down after foreseeing his assassination attempt.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the wedding day, Katakuri was on the roof of the Whole Cake Chateau as a man named <a href="/wiki/Jigra" title="Jigra">Jigra</a> attempted to get into the wedding without going through a body check. Katakuri, seeing that Jigra actually intended to take revenge on <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> and attack the venue, shot the man down as he was talking to <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>. Katakuri asked Bege if he thought it was wrong of him to do that and told him to tell Big Mom that it was his judgement to kill Jigra.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p><p>After the wedding began, Katakuri was eating and getting acquainted with some guests.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> While Pudding and Sanji stood on the altar, Katakuri foresaw Pudding breaking down in tears, much to his confusion. When that event happened, Big Mom signaled the priest to assassinate Sanji. Knowing that Sanji would dodge the shot, Katakuri tried to kill Sanji himself by launching a jellybean at him. However, to his surprise, Sanji managed to evade the attack and it hit the priest instead with Sanji glaring at Katakuri for his action. Having failed to kill Sanji, Katakuri then stood close to Big Mom, preparing for the chaos that was going to happen.<sup id="cite_ref-c862_30-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c862-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702160054" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Armament Haki Logia Form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri Armament Haki Logia Form.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702160054"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702160054" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Armament Haki Logia Form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702160054" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri Armament Haki Logia Form.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bc/Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702160054"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_Armament_Haki_Logia_Form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri restrains Luffy with his Devil Fruit powers and Armament Haki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As duplicates of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> were unleashed into the venue, the real Luffy attempted to break the photo of <a href="/wiki/Carmel" title="Carmel">Carmel</a>, but Katakuri stopped him with <a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">his Devil Fruit powers</a> and immobilized him. When Big Mom was accusing him of interfering with her business, Katakuri informed her of Luffy's intentions before demanding to know how Luffy knew about the photo. <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> then freed Luffy using black tea before claiming that he was the one who told Luffy about the photo.<sup id="cite_ref-c863_31-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863-31">[31]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the ensuing conflict, Katakuri foresaw a horrific future and approached Luffy and Bege. He ordered Bege to kill Luffy, but the latter outright refused before initiating his plot to assassinate Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-48">[48]</a></sup> As Katakuri went after Luffy, he told his older brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</a> to kill the captive <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>. Bege tried to hold Katakuri back by shooting him, but the bullets had no effect on him due to his Devil Fruit powers and Katakuri realized his treachery. He bypassed Bege as Jinbe and <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> tried to attack him, but he managed to get past them and used his ability to pin Luffy down. However, despite his efforts, Luffy managed to show Carmel's broken portrait to Big Mom, causing her to start screaming, which incapacitated Katakuri in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-c865_50-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c865-50">[50]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/The_Big_Mom_Pirates_confronts_the_Straw_Hat_and_Fire_Tank_Alliance.png/revision/latest?cb=20170612034527" class="image"><img alt="The Big Mom Pirates confronts the Straw Hat and Fire Tank Alliance" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/The_Big_Mom_Pirates_confronts_the_Straw_Hat_and_Fire_Tank_Alliance.png/revision/latest?cb=20170612034527" class="image"><img alt="The Big Mom Pirates confronts the Straw Hat and Fire Tank Alliance"
