decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Big Mom Pirates confronts the Straw Hat and Fire Tank Alliance.png" data-image-key="The_Big_Mom_Pirates_confronts_the_Straw_Hat_and_Fire_Tank_Alliance.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/The_Big_Mom_Pirates_confronts_the_Straw_Hat_and_Fire_Tank_Alliance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170612034527"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Big_Mom_Pirates_confronts_the_Straw_Hat_and_Fire_Tank_Alliance.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Big Mom Pirates confront the Straw Hat and Fire Tank Alliance.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Bege's assassination attempt failed, Katakuri created earplugs with his powers and distributed them to his siblings.<sup id="cite_ref-c868a_33-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868a-33">[33]</a></sup> They then surrounded Luffy, Bege and their allies before Bege transformed into a <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">giant fortress</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c868b_51-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c868b-51">[51]</a></sup> As Luffy's group and the Vinsmoke Family ran into the fortress, Katakuri used his ability and grabbed <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> from <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>'s back. He then used his jellybean bullets to attack several members of the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>. Katakuri later used his ability to plug the cannons in Bege's fortress, preventing them from firing at Big Mom. Waiting with his siblings for their enemies' next move, Katakuri remarked to Brûlée on how her captors used her in their plan, but she replied that she was the victim and told him to make their enemies pay.<sup id="cite_ref-c869b_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869b-39">[39]</a></sup> While the Straw Hats, Fire Tank Pirates and Vinsmoke Family were hiding inside Bege's fortress, Katakuri commented on how they made a mess of the wedding as Big Mom assaulted the fortress. Right after Bege deactivated his Big Father form and the Vinsmoke Family appeared, the Big Mom Pirates attacked them with a volley of bullets, but <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Vinsmoke Ichiji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Niji" title="Vinsmoke Niji">Vinsmoke Niji</a> blocked them with their capes.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702171730" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Defeats Ichiji" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="148" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri Defeats Ichiji.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702171730"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702171730" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Defeats Ichiji" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702171730" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="148" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri Defeats Ichiji.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702171730"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_Defeats_Ichiji.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri defeats Ichiji.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Caesar flew Bege away from the venue, Katakuri stood in their way. Ichiji leaped in and attacked Katakuri, but Katakuri used his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> power to split in two. He quickly defeated Ichiji, but as this happened, the <a href="/wiki/Tamatebako" title="Tamatebako">Tamatebako</a> exploded at the foot of the Whole Cake Chateau and caused it to topple.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_52-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-52">[52]</a></sup> The Big Mom Pirates were saved when <a href="/wiki/Streusen" title="Streusen">Streusen</a> used his Devil Fruit power to turn the whole castle into a cake. However, the Straw Hats, Bege's crew and the Vinsmokes escaped during the chateau's destruction. Katakuri then told his younger brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> to form two pursuit teams to go after the Straw Hats and Fire Tank Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-53">[53]</a></sup>
</p><p>Katakuri then stood with his siblings and crew, reflecting on the recent events to find answers. After solving a few of them, Katakuri was then told by Daifuku that the pursuit groups had assembled to go after the Straw Hats, Fire Tank Pirates and <a href="/wiki/Germa_Kingdom" title="Germa Kingdom">Germa</a>. Katakuri was pleased to hear this and told Brûlée to accompany him in pursuing the Straw Hats. He planned to kill Luffy before he could become a serious threat in the future. Before he could act, Katakuri was alerted by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Smoothie" title="Charlotte Smoothie">Charlotte Smoothie</a> to run and was shocked to see Big Mom rampaging through the city while holding <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Opera" title="Charlotte Opera">Charlotte Opera</a>. Katakuri watched as Perospero managed to get her attention and succeeded in luring her away to pursue the Straw Hats by promising another wedding cake. Katakuri began worrying about the island being destroyed after Big Mom realized Perospero's deception as Pudding arrived, promising to solve the problem by making another cake.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png/revision/latest?cb=20230211212821" class="image"><img alt="Luffy vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy vs. Katakuri.png" data-image-key="Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230211212821"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png/revision/latest?cb=20230211212821" class="image"><img alt="Luffy vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230211212821" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy vs. Katakuri.png" data-image-key="Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230211212821"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_vs._Katakuri.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri clashes with Luffy as the Straw Hats try taking back the Sunny.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Using Brûlée's ability to <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">travel through mirrors</a>, Katakuri and several subordinates infiltrated the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>. Despite believing that being chased by Linlin herself meant that the Straw Hat Pirates would have absolutely no chance of escaping alive, Katakuri nevertheless decided to wait for the Straw Hats onboard their ship so he could ambush them should they return.<sup id="cite_ref-c874_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c874-21">[21]</a></sup> He was later joined by Perospero when <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> returned to the ship with the <a href="/wiki/Shark_Submerge_III" title="Shark Submerge III">Shark Submerge III</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c875_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c875-54">[54]</a></sup> While Brook and Chopper fought the Chess Soldiers on the Sunny's deck, Katakuri simply stood back and commented on Brook's strength.<sup id="cite_ref-c876_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c876-55">[55]</a></sup> Perospero then immobilized the two Straw Hats and prepared to turn them into candy, but Katakuri noticed that Big Mom was coming and still chasing after the Straw Hats. Katakuri then ordered the Big Mom Pirates on the ship to retreat, having foreseen that Luffy would defeat them.<sup id="cite_ref-c877a_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877a-44">[44]</a></sup> After Perospero failed to block the Straw Hats' path, Luffy came in and attacked, but Katakuri parried his punch. The two began fighting for the ship, and Katakuri eventually managed to catch Luffy's arm and then hit him with a <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a>-clad punch.<sup id="cite_ref-c877b_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c877b-71">[71]</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> engulfed Perospero in his suicidal explosion, Katakuri worried for his brother and was in disbelief at the event. When the Sanji Retrieval Team made final preparations for their getaway, Katakuri charged at them while <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> attempted to attack Katakuri, but he easily subdued her. Luffy then grabbed the Sweet Commander and dragged him into the Mirro-World. Once there, he complimented Luffy's strategy as Luffy smashed the mirror to the Sunny and the two stared each other down as they prepared to continue their fight.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a9/Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172200" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri vs. Luffy Elephant Gun.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a9/Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172200"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a9/Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172200" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a9/Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172200" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri vs. Luffy Elephant Gun.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a9/Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172200"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_vs._Luffy_Elephant_Gun.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri and Luffy clash inside the Mirro-World.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the Sunny fled from Big Mom and her fleet, Luffy and Katakuri commenced their fight, with Katakuri claiming that he had Luffy outmatched in both speed and power. After Luffy attacked with <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques#Haki_Enhanced_Attacks" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Hawk Gatling</a>, Katakuri countered with several mochi tendrils hardened into fists, before proceeding to warn Luffy that anything Luffy could do, he could do it better. Luffy then asserted that rubber would never lose to mochi, but his subsequent Hawk Stamp was dodged and Katakuri kicked him into a wall. Luffy then tried using <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques#Post-Timeskip" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques">Elephant Gun</a>, but Katakuri created an even larger fist and pushed Luffy into the wall with tremendous power, overwhelming Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c879b_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c879b-58">[58]</a></sup>
</p><p>With Luffy lying on the floor, Katakuri made contact with Perospero (who survived the explosion) and confirmed the situation with Big Mom and the other Straw Hats. Katakuri then ordered Brûlée to find another mirror on the Sunny and use the portal to set the Sunny on fire. After <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Joscarpone" title="Charlotte Joscarpone">Charlotte Joscarpone</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Mascarpone" title="Charlotte Mascarpone">Charlotte Mascarpone</a> arrived with a mirror, Luffy rushed towards them, but Katakuri stopped him and reminded him of his promise to fight one-on-one. Katakuri then resumed attacking Luffy, warning him not to lay a hand on his younger brothers and sisters.<sup id="cite_ref-c880_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c880-36">[36]</a></sup> After overpowering Luffy, Katakuri was told by Perospero that Big Mom sunk the Thousand Sunny. As his siblings were puzzled by the mirrors to the Sunny breaking one after another, Katakuri noticed Luffy running away. Katakuri then further assaulted Luffy and prepared to kill him.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup> As Katakuri continued to have the upper hand, Brûlée taunted Luffy by boasting of her brother's reputation of the perfect being. Luffy then tried to punch her, but Katakuri grabbed his fist and slammed him into a wall. After pondering on how he should maim Luffy, Katakuri then began to attack with his trident <a href="/wiki/Mogura" title="Mogura">Mogura</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c882b_40-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882b-40">[40]</a></sup> In the midst of this, Katakuri noted how Luffy dodged his strikes more so than anyone and revealed his awakened powers to trap the Straw Hat captain.<sup id="cite_ref-c882c_59-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c882c-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png/revision/latest?cb=20181007180541" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Sees Katakuri Eating" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="194" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Sees Katakuri Eating.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181007180541"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png/revision/latest?cb=20181007180541" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Sees Katakuri Eating" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181007180541" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="194" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Sees Katakuri Eating.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181007180541"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Sees_Katakuri_Eating.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Luffy intrudes on Katakuri's snack time.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Luffy was restrained, he prepared to resort to using <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Gear 4</a>, but Katakuri had no desire to watch him power up and prevented Luffy from activating it by engulfing him with mochi. Growing tired of their battle making his snack time late, Katakuri turned much of the surrounding Mirro-World into mochi and piled it onto Luffy in order to suffocate him. Believing that their battle was finished, Katakuri called his three chefs, who arrived to bring Katakuri's snack to him. Katakuri then created a mochi house to consume his sweet treats and iced tea in private.<sup id="cite_ref-c883c_46-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883c-46">[46]</a></sup> As he gorged on giant doughnuts, Luffy broke into his house after eating his way out of the mochi and saw him in the state of eating.<sup id="cite_ref-c883a_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883a-8">[8]</a></sup> This made Katakuri furious and he quickly dispatched his chefs before attacking Luffy,<sup id="cite_ref-c883d_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883d-47">[47]</a></sup> overwhelming him with strong <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c883f_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883f-79">[79]</a></sup> However, Luffy managed to land a kick on Katakuri's jaw, and Katakuri was incredulous when Luffy stated he had figured out his weakness. Luffy then activated Gear 4 and struck Katakuri with Kong Gun, which Katakuri blocked.<sup id="cite_ref-c883e_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c883e-60">[60]</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy gained the upper hand against Katakuri, landing several Gear 4 attacks on him. However, once Katakuri regained his composure, he resumed dodging Luffy's attacks and landed a powerful strike on Luffy, knocking him back.<sup id="cite_ref-c884_61-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c884-61">[61]</a></sup> Having the advantage again, Katakuri went on the offensive, but when he mentioned that Luffy would deflate, Luffy realized that his Gear 4 would wear out soon and retreated. Katakuri chased after Luffy as he was fleeing after his Gear 4 wore out. Unfortunately for Katakuri, Luffy came across Brûlée, grabbed her, and escaped the Mirro-World, leaving Katakuri behind before he could catch him.<sup id="cite_ref-c885_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c885-62">[62]</a></sup> He later wandered the Mirro-World, searching for any signs of Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c886_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c886-63">[63]</a></sup> Eventually, Luffy returned to confront Katakuri and they clashed once again.<sup id="cite_ref-c888_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c888-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220722180107" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Wounds Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri Wounds Luffy.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220722180107"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220722180107" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Wounds Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220722180107" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri Wounds Luffy.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220722180107"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_Wounds_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri strikes Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Though Katakuri pummeled Luffy many times, the latter kept getting back up. When Luffy attempted to counter against his giant mochi fist, Katakuri noticed that Luffy was beginning to see into the future just like him. He then tried to deter Luffy from continuing the fight, but Luffy refused to give up.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup> Knowing that Luffy's Observation Haki was improving, Katakuri tried to end the battle quickly and used his <b>Mochi Tsuki</b> to deal a devastating blow to Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c892_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c892-64">[64]</a></sup> Unbeknownst to Katakuri, Luffy's focus was broken after he was shot in the leg by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Flampe" title="Charlotte Flampe">Charlotte Flampe</a>, and the Sweet Commander took advantage of this as he pummeled Luffy. Suspicious of Luffy's sudden loss of focus, Katakuri heard Flampe's laughing and realized what had happened. He approached her and while Flampe was flying towards him in joy, Katakuri stabbed himself with Mogura in the same place he stabbed Luffy. He then removed his scarf and loudly berated her for interfering in his fight. Distraught, Flampe began mocking his mouth and told her subordinates to photograph him, but Katakuri paid little mind to them as he returned to face Luffy.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20230703130830" class="image"><img alt="Luffy and Katakuri's Final Clash" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy and Katakuri's Final Clash.png" data-image-key="Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230703130830"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20230703130830" class="image"><img alt="Luffy and Katakuri's Final Clash" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230703130830" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy and Katakuri's Final Clash.png" data-image-key="Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/91/Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230703130830"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_and_Katakuri%27s_Final_Clash.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri and Luffy meet in a final clash.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two unleashed a wave of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, knocking out Flampe and her subordinates. Katakuri prepared to resume fighting Luffy, now thinking of him as an equal.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup> They continued to trade blows with each other and as they were getting worn out from the battle, Katakuri watched as Luffy activated another variation of Gear 4: <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques#Snakeman" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Snakeman</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> With his increased speed and ability to home in on his target, Luffy was able to land more hits on Katakuri. However, Katakuri countered with his spiked mochi attacks. After trading more blows with each other, both fighters claimed that they would end the battle before engaging in a massive clash.<sup id="cite_ref-c895_73-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c895-73">[73]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 224px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172410" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Defeats Katakuri" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="224" height="126" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Defeats Katakuri.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20230702172410"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172410" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Defeats Katakuri" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20230702172410" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="224" height="126" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Defeats Katakuri.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20230702172410"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Defeats_Katakuri.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri defeated.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the clash, Luffy's Gear 4 wore off and he fell down as the floor collapsed under him from the impact of Katakuri's attack, right before Katakuri collapsed. As Luffy later climbed out of the hole, Katakuri briefly stood up and asked Luffy if he would return to defeat Big Mom. Luffy replied that he would in order to become the Pirate King. Amused by this answer, Katakuri commented on this by saying that Luffy was looking pretty far into the future and once again collapsed and fell unconscious. Defeated, his mouth was covered by Luffy before the Straw Hat captain departed.<sup id="cite_ref-c896_27-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-27">[27]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172548" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri's Wounds" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="217" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri's Wounds.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172548"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172548" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri's Wounds" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172548" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="217" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri's Wounds.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172548"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée tends to Katakuri's wounds.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He later woke up with Brûlée beside him tending to his wounds. She took notice that he intentionally fell on his back and Katakuri confessed that the rumor of him never lying on his back was false. She then admitted that she always knew the truth as she had seen him through the mirrors. Katakuri asked her what became of the Straw Hats and he smirked after she explained that they escaped their territory.<sup id="cite_ref-c902a_23-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902a-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span></h3>
<h4><span id="Germa_66.27s_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Germa_66's_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion">Germa 66's Ahh... An Emotionless Excursion</span></h4>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">Vinsmoke Reiju</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Vinsmoke Ichiji</a> broke into the laboratory on <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island" title="Whole Cake Island">Whole Cake Island</a> and freed <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Niji" title="Vinsmoke Niji">Vinsmoke Niji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Vinsmoke Yonji</a>, Katakuri and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a> arrived and attacked the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmokes</a>. However, <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> released a <a href="/wiki/Gasu_Gasu_no_Mi" title="Gasu Gasu no Mi">gas cloud</a> <sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup>, which caused Katakuri and Oven to hallucinate and fight each other.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Red">One Piece Film: Red</span></h4>
<p>Katakuri volunteered to go to <a href="/wiki/Elegia" title="Elegia">Elegia</a> to rescue <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a> from <a href="/wiki/Uta" title="Uta">Uta</a>'s concert. In order to save his siblings, he reluctantly teamed up with the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> and the Marines to battle <a href="/wiki/Tot_Musica" title="Tot Musica">Tot Musica</a> while the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> attacked the creature from within the <a href="/wiki/Uta_World" title="Uta World">Uta World</a>.
</p><p>After the events of Elegia, Katakuri, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Pudding</a> and Brûlée listened to Uta's childhood song <a href="/wiki/Where_the_Wind_Blows" title="Where the Wind Blows">Where the Wind Blows</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Dials#Tone_Dial" title="Dials">Tone Dial</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr></small><small></small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p><small><hr></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png/revision/latest?cb=20240630150943" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom Pirates View Broadcast" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Big Mom Pirates View Broadcast.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240630150943"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png/revision/latest?cb=20240630150943" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom Pirates View Broadcast" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240630150943" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Big Mom Pirates View Broadcast.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240630150943"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Big_Mom_Pirates_View_Broadcast.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Katakuri views the broadcast on Whole Cake Island.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Some time later, Katakuri watched <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s broadcast to the world alongside his siblings.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span></h2>
<p>Katakuri is given an earlier introduction in the anime where he was shown arriving at the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a>. In the manga, he was first shown at the opening of the <a href="/wiki/Tea_Party" title="Tea Party">Tea Party</a>. 
</p><p>Katakuri's <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a> while performing Zan Giri Mochi does not have the light blue luster in the anime as it does in the manga. In the anime, it is a regular dark blue luster like most characters.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li>Katakuri's name is based on the Japanese name of "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Erythronium_japonicum" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Erythronium japonicum">Erythronium japonicum</a>", <i>katakuri</i> (片栗/カタクリ). The bulbs of said plant are used to make <i>katakuriko</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">片栗粉</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, a type of starch powder used for cooking. This follows the food-themed names of the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a> and <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>. This also is connected to his title, Minister of Flour, as starch powders are considered a type of flour.
<ul><li>Currently, most of the <i>katakuriko</i> available commercially are made of potato rather than genuine <i>katakuri</i> starch, so it's often understood to be "potato starch".</li></ul></li>
<li>Katakuri's incredible power, extreme gluttonous side, hair color and scarred mouth is similar to <a href="https://toriko.fandom.com/wiki/Zebra" class="extiw" title="w:c:toriko:Zebra">Zebra</a> from the <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toriko" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Toriko">Toriko</a></i> series.
<ul><li>Katakuri also shares two notable traits with two other characters that his Japanese voice actor <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tomokazu_Sugita" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tomokazu Sugita">Tomokazu Sugita</a> also happens to voice.
<ul><li>First off is <a href="https://jojo.fandom.com/wiki/Joseph_Joestar" class="extiw" title="w:c:jojo:Joseph Joestar">Joseph Joestar</a> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JoJo%27s_Bizarre_Adventure_(season_1)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:JoJo's Bizarre Adventure (season 1)">JoJo's Bizarre Adventure: Battle Tendency</a></i>, who also possesses the ability to predict what his opponents will say as a recurring gag.</li>
<li>Second is <a href="https://gintama.fandom.com/wiki/Sakata_Gintoki" class="extiw" title="w:c:gintama:Sakata Gintoki">Sakata Gintoki</a> from <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gintama" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Gintama">Gintama</a></i>, who is known for his massive sweet-tooth.</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>Katakuri's style of clothing may be inspired by American biker gang fashion, which is often distinguished by its usage of cropped leather vests, tattoos, belts, and decorative motorcyclist spurs.</li>
<li>Katakuri was originally meant to have the powers of the <b>Kona Kona no Mi</b>, a <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a> <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allowed him to turn into flour. This was eventually changed into the <a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">Mochi Mochi no Mi</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia#Special_Paramecia" title="Paramecia">special Paramecia</a> that turns the user into mochi instead. Katakuri holding the position of <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>'s Minister of Flour may have been a remnant of this concept.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>"<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Merienda" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Merienda">Merienda</a>", also known as "Merenda", is a real-life light meal that is popularized in southern Europe, particularly Spain, Portugal, Brazil, Italy as well as Hispanic America and the Philippines. Usually taken in the afternoon or for brunch, it fills in the meal gap between the noontime meal and the evening meal, being the equivalent of afternoon tea in the English-speaking world (mainly with the United Kingdom) or between breakfast and lunch.</li>
<li>In the seventh <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">popularity poll</a>, Katakuri ranked at 14th place, making him the most popular member of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a> as well as the most popular antagonist in the poll.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span></h3>
<ul><li>Katakuri's birthday, November 25, comes from a fan suggestion: 11 from ii, 2 from ni, and 5 from o, meaning "Three good big brothers"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">イイお兄さん三つ子</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><b>Ī</b> O<b>nī</b>san Mitsug<b>o</b></span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. He shares his birthday with his brothers, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs88_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs88-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>In order to never reveal his split mouth, Katakuri simply eats so fast in the presence of others that they cannot see.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs88_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs88-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>To maintain his image of "strength" (of his back having never touched the ground), Katakuri sleeps leaning on walls or sitting down.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs89_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs89-93">[93]</a></sup></li>
<li>Katakuri was ranked by his younger siblings as their favorite older brother.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs89_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs89-93">[93]</a></sup></li>
<li>Katakuri's favorite food are <a href="/wiki/Foods#Doughnuts" title="Foods">doughnuts</a> and his least favorite is hot <a href="/wiki/Foods#Ramen" title="Foods">ramen</a>, but he does not dislike spicy food.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs89_93-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs89-93">[93]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup></li></ul>
